‚úÖ JavaScript Basics
### _#01._ üü° What is JavaScript and why is it used?

JavaScript ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶ö-‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞, ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶° (Node.js ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá) ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#02._ üü° What is the difference between JavaScript and other programming languages?

JavaScript ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Python ‡¶¨‡¶æ Java ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏, ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá C++ ‡¶¨‡¶æ Java ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, Node.js ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#03._ üü° What is the difference between null, undefined, and NaN?

- **null**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x = null;`  
- **undefined**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x;`  
- **NaN**: "Not-a-Number" ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `0 / 0` ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `NaN` ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#04._ üü° What is the difference between var, let, and const?

- **var**: ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™‡¶°, ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **let**: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™‡¶°, ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
- **const**: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™‡¶°, ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶£ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const obj = {}; obj.key = 'value';`

### _#05._ üü° What is scope in JavaScript?

‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞:  
- **‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™**: ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§  
- **‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™**: ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§  
- **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™**: `{}` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß (let/const ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá)‡•§  
‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÉ‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#06._ üü° What is lexical scope?

‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶£ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

‚úÖ Functions and Execution
### _#07._ üü° What is a function and how does it work?

‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶´ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞) ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ (‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ) ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º `function` ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function add(a, b) { return a + b; }`‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `add(2, 3)`, ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø 5 ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§

### _#08._ üü° What is the difference between a regular function and an arrow function?

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:  
- **‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®**: `function` ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ `this` ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function myFunc() {}`  
- **‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®**: ES6-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏ (`() => {}`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ `this` ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ (‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤ `this` ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá), ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const myFunc = () => {};`  
‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `arguments` ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### _#09._ üü° What is a callback function and how does it work?

‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ API ‡¶ï‡¶≤, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `setTimeout(() => { console.log("Delayed"); }, 1000);` ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡ßß ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßÇ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#10._ üü° What is a higher-order function?

‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `Array.map()` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: `const numbers = [1, 2, 3]; const doubled = numbers.map(num => num * 2);` ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `map` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶É‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#11._ üü° What is closure in JavaScript and how does it work?

‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶£ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function outer() {
  let count = 0;
  return function inner() {
    count++;
    return count;
  };
}
const counter = outer();
console.log(counter()); // 1
console.log(counter()); // 2
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `inner` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® `count` ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶´‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‚úÖ Behind the Scenes
### _#12._ üü° How does JavaScript work behind the scenes?

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single-threaded, non-blocking ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ V8 engine (Chrome-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø execution-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º call stack, heap, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event loop ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Code execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:  
1. **Call Stack**: Function calls track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
2. **Heap**: Objects ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamic data store ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
3. **Event Loop**: Asynchronous tasks (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® setTimeout, API calls) manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
JavaScript code parse ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá abstract syntax tree (AST) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ bytecode-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Engine ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç asynchronous operations Web APIs (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® DOM, fetch) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá handle ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Event loop callback queue ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá tasks ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá call stack-‡¶è push ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#13._ üü° What is the call stack and event loop?

- **Call Stack**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø data structure ‡¶Ø‡¶æ function execution-‡¶è‡¶∞ track ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ stack-‡¶è push ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç execution ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá pop ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function a() { b(); } function b() {}` ‡¶è `a` call ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá stack-‡¶è `a`, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ `b` ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
- **Event Loop**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø asynchronous tasks manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Call stack ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, event loop callback queue (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® setTimeout-‡¶è‡¶∞ callbacks) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá tasks ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá stack-‡¶è push ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Web APIs ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript runtime-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `setTimeout(() => console.log('Hi'), 1000)` ‡ßß ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶∞ callback queue-‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event loop ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#14._ üü° What is the difference between synchronous and asynchronous code?

- **Synchronous Code**: Line-by-line execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø operation ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø wait ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x = 1; console.log(x);` ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßé‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Synchronous code blocking ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ performance-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Asynchronous Code**: Operations simultaneously ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç result-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø wait ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ code execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `setTimeout(() => console.log('Async'), 0);` ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá callback queue-‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Async code non-blocking, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ API calls ‡¶¨‡¶æ I/O operations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ Promises, async/await ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç callbacks async code handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#15._ üü° What is the event loop, microtask, and macrotask?

- **Event Loop**: JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ mechanism ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous tasks coordinate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Call stack ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø microtask queue ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç macrotask queue ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá tasks ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Microtask**: High-priority tasks, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Promise resolutions ‡¶¨‡¶æ `queueMicrotask`‡•§ Microtasks macrotasks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `Promise.resolve().then(() => console.log('Microtask'));`  
- **Macrotask**: Lower-priority tasks, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `setTimeout`, `setInterval`, ‡¶¨‡¶æ I/O events‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã task queue-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `setTimeout(() => console.log('Macrotask'), 0);`  
Event loop ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá microtask queue ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø macrotask execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á cycle ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: Promise-‡¶è‡¶∞ `.then` microtask ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ `setTimeout` macrotask ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‚úÖ Hoisting, this, and Object-related
### _#16._ üü° What is hoisting in JavaScript?

Hoisting ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø behavior ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá variable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function declarations execution-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ scope-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá "hoisted" ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶†‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `console.log(x); var x = 5;` ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `undefined` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ `var x` hoisted ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ initialization ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Function declarations ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø hoisted ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: `foo(); function foo() { console.log('Hi'); }` ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `let` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `const` hoisted ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ temporal dead zone-‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á initialization-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá error ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#17._ üü° What is the "this" keyword and how does it work in different contexts?

`this` keyword ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reference ‡¶Ø‡¶æ execution context-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® context-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:  
- **Global Context**: Browser-‡¶è `this` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã `window` object‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `console.log(this); // window`  
- **Function Context**: Regular function-‡¶è `this` global object (non-strict mode) ‡¶¨‡¶æ `undefined` (strict mode)‡•§  
- **Object Method**: Object-‡¶è‡¶∞ method-‡¶è `this` ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á object-‡¶ï‡ßá point ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const obj = { name: 'Test', getName() { return this.name; } }; console.log(obj.getName()); // Test`  
- **Constructor**: `new` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá call ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `this` ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® object-‡¶ï‡ßá point ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Arrow Function**: `this` lexical scope ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ `this` ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
`call`, `apply`, `bind` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá `this` explicitly set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#18._ üü° What is the "new" keyword in JavaScript?

`new` keyword ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è object creation-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø constructor function ‡¶¨‡¶æ class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:  
1. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø empty object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
2. `this` ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á object-‡¶è bind ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
3. Object-‡¶è‡¶∞ prototype constructor-‡¶è‡¶∞ prototype-‡¶è link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
4. Constructor function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç object return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function Person(name) { this.name = name; } const person = new Person('John'); console.log(person.name); // John`

### _#19._ üü° What is a constructor function?

Constructor function ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø special function ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `new` keyword-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø object-‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods initialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Convention ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ, constructor-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ Capital letter ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function Car(model) {
  this.model = model;
  this.drive = function() { console.log('Driving'); };
}
const myCar = new Car('Toyota');
console.log(myCar.model); // Toyota
```
Constructor functions prototypal inheritance-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ES6-‡¶è class syntax ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ alternative‡•§

### _#20._ üü° What is prototypal inheritance?

Prototypal inheritance ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø mechanism ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá objects ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø objects ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø object-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø prototype ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø object ‡¶¨‡¶æ `null` ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã property ‡¶¨‡¶æ method object-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá prototype-‡¶è ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
const parent = { greet: () => console.log('Hello'); };
const child = Object.create(parent);
child.greet(); // Hello
```
ES6 classes ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `extends` prototypal inheritance implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#21._ üü° What is the prototype chain?

Prototype chain ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø process ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø object-‡¶è‡¶∞ property ‡¶¨‡¶æ method ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ prototype-‡¶è ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø prototype-‡¶è‡¶∞ prototype-‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ `null` ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
const obj = {};
console.log(obj.toString()); // [object Object]
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `toString` `obj`-‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á prototype (`Object.prototype`) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Chain ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º `Object.prototype`-‡¶è, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ prototype `null`‡•§

### _#22._ üü° What is the difference between primitive and reference types?

- **Primitive Types**: Simple, immutable data types ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `number`, `string`, `boolean`, `null`, `undefined`, `symbol`, `bigint`‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã memory-‡¶§‡ßá directly value store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x = 5; let y = x; y = 10; console.log(x); // 5`  
- **Reference Types**: Objects (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `object`, `array`, `function`) ‡¶Ø‡¶æ memory-‡¶§‡ßá reference store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reference ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá original object ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let arr1 = [1, 2]; let arr2 = arr1; arr2.push(3); console.log(arr1); // [1, 2, 3]`  
Primitive copy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º value ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá, reference copy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º reference ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡•§

### _#23._ üü° What is call by value and call by reference?

- **Call by Value**: Primitive types function-‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ value copy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Function-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® original value-‡¶ï‡ßá affect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function change(num) { num = 10; }
let x = 5;
change(x);
console.log(x); // 5
```  
- **Call by Reference**: Reference types (objects) pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ reference copy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Function-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® original object-‡¶ï‡ßá affect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function changeObj(obj) { obj.key = 'new'; }
let myObj = { key: 'old' };
changeObj(myObj);
console.log(myObj.key); // new
```  
JavaScript technically call by value-‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá value ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã reference‡•§

‚úÖ Control Flow
### _#24._ üü° What is an if-else statement and how does it work?

If-else statement ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø control flow structure ‡¶Ø‡¶æ condition-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá code execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø condition true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá `if` block-‡¶è‡¶∞ code ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá; ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º `else` block (‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá) ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Nested if-else ‡¶¨‡¶æ else-if ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
let num = 10;
if (num > 0) {
  console.log('Positive');
} else if (num < 0) {
  console.log('Negative');
} else {
  console.log('Zero');
}
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `num > 0` true ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º 'Positive' ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ If-else decision-making ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç conditional logic-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#25._ üü° What is a switch statement?

Switch statement ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø control flow structure ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø expression-‡¶è‡¶∞ value-‡¶ï‡ßá multiple case-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø case matching value-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü code block execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `break` ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ case-‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º (fall-through)‡•§ `default` block optional, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã case match ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
let day = 'Monday';
switch (day) {
  case 'Monday':
    console.log('Start of week');
    break;
  case 'Friday':
    console.log('End of week');
    break;
  default:
    console.log('Regular day');
}
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá 'Start of week' ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### _#26._ üü° What is the difference between if-else and switch?

- **If-else**: Multiple conditions check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® range, complex logic (>, <, &&, ||)‡•§ Flexible ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ lengthy code-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø complex ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `if (x > 10 && x < 20)`‡•§  
- **Switch**: Single expression-‡¶è‡¶∞ exact value match ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ Cleaner syntax ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® fixed values compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Fall-through behavior ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `break` ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  
If-else ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø versatile, switch specific cases-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø efficient‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: Days of week-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø switch ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ range-based conditions-‡¶è if-else ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

### _#27._ üü° What is a loop? (for, while, do-while)

Loop ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø structure ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code block-‡¶ï‡ßá repeated execution-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ condition true ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® loop:  
- **For Loop**: Fixed number of iterations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Syntax: `for (initialization; condition; update)`‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) { console.log(i); }` // 0, 1, 2, 3, 4  
- **While Loop**: Condition true ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá, iteration count unknown ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let i = 0; while (i < 5) { console.log(i); i++; }`  
- **Do-While Loop**: Condition check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let i = 0; do { console.log(i); i++; } while (i < 5);`  
Loops repetitive tasks ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#28._ üü° What is the difference between a for loop and a while loop?

- **For Loop**: Initialization, condition, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á line-‡¶è define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Known number of iterations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ideal‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) { console.log(i); }`‡•§ Compact ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable‡•§  
- **While Loop**: ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ condition check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, initialization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update separately handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Unknown iterations ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex conditions-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let i = 0; while (i < 5) { console.log(i); i++; }`  
For loop predictable iterations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, while loop dynamic ‡¶¨‡¶æ conditional iterations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø suitable‡•§ Both ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ syntax ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç use case ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§

‚úÖ Modern JavaScript (ES6+)
### _#29._ üü° What is destructuring?

Destructuring ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ array ‡¶¨‡¶æ object ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá values extract ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá variables-‡¶è assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø code-‡¶ï‡ßá concise ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Array Destructuring**: ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const [a, b] = [1, 2]; console.log(a, b); // 1, 2`  
- **Object Destructuring**: ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const { name, age } = { name: 'John', age: 30 }; console.log(name, age); // John, 30`  
Nested destructuring, default values, ‡¶¨‡¶æ rest operator ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const { name = 'Unknown' } = {};`‡•§

### _#30._ üü° What is the rest operator and spread operator?

- **Rest Operator**: `...` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá function parameters ‡¶¨‡¶æ destructuring-‡¶è remaining elements collect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function sum(...numbers) { return numbers.reduce((a, b) => a + b); } console.log(sum(1, 2, 3)); // 6`‡•§ Destructuring-‡¶è: `const [a, ...rest] = [1, 2, 3]; console.log(rest); // [2, 3]`  
- **Spread Operator**: `...` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá array ‡¶¨‡¶æ object-‡¶è‡¶∞ elements spread ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const arr1 = [1, 2]; const arr2 = [...arr1, 3]; console.log(arr2); // [1, 2, 3]`‡•§ Object-‡¶è: `const obj1 = { a: 1 }; const obj2 = { ...obj1, b: 2 }; console.log(obj2); // { a: 1, b: 2 }`  
Rest collects, spread expands‡•§

### _#31._ üü° What is the difference between == and ===?

- **== (Loose Equality)**: Type coercion ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá values compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `5 == '5'; // true` ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ string '5' number-‡¶è convert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
- **=== (Strict Equality)**: Type coercion ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ value ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `5 === '5'; // false` ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ types ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§  
Strict equality (`===`) safer ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç predictable, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á usually ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `!=` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `!==` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#32._ üü° What are template literals?

Template literals ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ string creation-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Backticks (\`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá strings define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `${}` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá expressions embed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Multi-line strings ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
const name = 'John';
const greeting = `Hello, ${name}! 
This is a multi-line string.`;
console.log(greeting); // Hello, John! This is a multi-line string.
```
Traditional string concatenation-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º template literals cleaner ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible‡•§

### _#33._ üü° What are ES6 classes?

ES6 classes ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è object-oriented programming-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø syntactic sugar‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø constructor functions ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç prototypal inheritance-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Class-‡¶è `constructor`, methods, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inheritance (`extends`) define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
class Person {
  constructor(name) {
    this.name = name;
  }
  greet() {
    console.log(`Hi, I'm ${this.name}`);
  }
}
class Student extends Person {
  constructor(name, grade) {
    super(name);
    this.grade = grade;
  }
}
const student = new Student('John', 'A');
student.greet(); // Hi, I'm John
```
Classes cleaner syntax ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ internally prototypes-‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#34._ üü° What are arrow functions?

Arrow functions ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø concise syntax (`=>`) ‡¶Ø‡¶æ regular functions-‡¶è‡¶∞ alternative‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø:  
- ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ `this` ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, lexical `this` inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- Shorter syntax‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const add = (a, b) => a + b;`  
- `return` implicit ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá single expression-‡¶è‡•§  
- Constructor ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const obj = { name: 'John', sayHi: () => console.log(this.name) }; obj.sayHi(); // undefined (this is window)`‡•§ Callbacks ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functional programming-‡¶è popular‡•§

### _#35._ üü° What are default parameters?

Default parameters ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6-‡¶è‡¶∞ feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ function parameters-‡¶è default values set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø argument pass ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, default value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function greet(name = 'Guest') {
  return `Hello, ${name}`;
}
console.log(greet()); // Hello, Guest
console.log(greet('John')); // Hello, John
```
Default parameters code-‡¶ï‡ßá robust ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç undefined checks ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#36._ üü° What is immutability in JavaScript?

Immutability ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá data ‡¶Ø‡¶æ create ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ JavaScript-‡¶è primitive types (string, number) immutable, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ objects ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç arrays mutable‡•§ Immutable data predictable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç side effects ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Immutability achieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá:  
- `const` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ (‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ reassignment ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá)‡•§  
- Spread operator: `const newArr = [...arr];`  
- Libraries ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Immutable.js ‡¶¨‡¶æ deep-freeze‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const obj = { a: 1 }; Object.freeze(obj); obj.a = 2; console.log(obj.a); // 1`‡•§ Functional programming-‡¶è immutability ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

### _#37._ üü° What are map(), filter(), and reduce()?

`map()`, `filter()`, `reduce()` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã array methods ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional programming-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:  
- **map()**: Array-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element transform ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá new array return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const arr = [1, 2, 3]; const doubled = arr.map(x => x * 2); // [2, 4, 6]`  
- **filter()**: Condition match ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ new array return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const evens = arr.filter(x => x % 2 === 0); // [2]`  
- **reduce()**: Array-‡¶ï‡ßá single value-‡¶è reduce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const sum = arr.reduce((acc, curr) => acc + curr, 0); // 6`  
‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã original array modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, immutable way-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‚úÖ DOM & Browser
### _#38._ üü° What is the DOM and how does JavaScript interact with it?

DOM (Document Object Model) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø programming interface ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML ‡¶¨‡¶æ XML document-‡¶ï‡ßá tree structure ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø node‡•§ JavaScript DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interact ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web page-‡¶è‡¶∞ content, structure, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç style dynamically manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
- **Access**: `document.getElementById('id')` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `querySelector('.class')` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá elements select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- **Modify**: `element.innerHTML = 'New Content';` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `element.style.color = 'red';`  
- **Events**: `element.addEventListener('click', () => console.log('Clicked'));`  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `document.querySelector('p').textContent = 'Hello';` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø paragraph-‡¶è‡¶∞ text change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript DOM API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá web page interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#39._ üü° What is event bubbling?

Event bubbling ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø mechanism ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø event child element-‡¶è trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ parent elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá upward propagate ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
<div onclick="console.log('Div')">
  <button onclick="console.log('Button')">Click</button>
</div>
```
Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá 'Button', ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ 'Div' ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Event bubbling default behavior‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø stop ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `event.stopPropagation()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Bubbling event listeners manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event delegation-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#40._ üü° What is event delegation?

Event delegation ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø technique ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá individual child elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá parent element-‡¶è single event listener set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event bubbling-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá child elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø memory-efficient ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamically added elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
document.querySelector('ul').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
  if (e.target.tagName === 'LI') {
    console.log(e.target.textContent);
  }
});
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `ul`-‡¶è listener ‡¶∏‡¶¨ `li`-‡¶è‡¶∞ click handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `e.target` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá specific element identify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#41._ üü° What are setTimeout and setInterval?

- **setTimeout**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function-‡¶ï‡ßá specified delay (milliseconds-‡¶è) ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
setTimeout(() => console.log('Delayed'), 1000); // 1 ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶∞ 'Delayed' ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü
```
Clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá: `clearTimeout(timeoutId);`  
- **setInterval**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function-‡¶ï‡ßá repeatedly ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü interval (milliseconds-‡¶è) ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
setInterval(() => console.log('Every 2s'), 2000); // ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡ß® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü
```
Clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá: `clearInterval(intervalId);`  

‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á asynchronous, Web APIs ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá handle ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event loop-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá callback execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Timing animations, polling, ‡¶¨‡¶æ delayed tasks-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§

‚úÖ Asynchronous JavaScript
### _#42._ üü° What is a promise and how does it work?

Promise ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø object ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous operation-‡¶è‡¶∞ eventual completion ‡¶¨‡¶æ failure represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø callback hell ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Promise-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø state:  
- **Pending**: Operation ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  
- **Fulfilled**: Operation successful‡•§  
- **Rejected**: Operation failed‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
const promise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  setTimeout(() => resolve('Success'), 1000);
});
promise.then(result => console.log(result)) // Success
       .catch(error => console.log(error));
```
`.then()` success handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, `.catch()` error handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Promises chain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Promise.all()`, `Promise.race()` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#43._ üü° What is async/await?

Async/await ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6-‡¶è‡¶∞ syntactic sugar ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Promises-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì readable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç synchronous-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã asynchronous code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **`async`**: Function-‡¶ï‡ßá async ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Promise return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **`await`**: Promise resolve/reject ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ wait ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
async function fetchData() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('https://api.example.com/data');
    const data = await response.json();
    console.log(data);
  } catch (error) {
    console.log('Error:', error);
  }
}
fetchData();
```
`await` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `async` function-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø cleaner code ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç error handling-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Async/await internally Promises-‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#44._ üü° What is try/catch and how is it used for error handling?

Try/catch ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ error handling mechanism ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code execution-‡¶è potential errors manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `try` block-‡¶è risky code ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `catch` block-‡¶è error handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Optional `finally` block always execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
try {
  const result = JSON.parse('invalid json');
  console.log(result);
} catch (error) {
  console.log('Error:', error.message);
} finally {
  console.log('Cleanup');
}
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `try` fail ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `catch` error ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `finally` ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Try/catch synchronous ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç async (with `try/catch`) code-‡¶è error handling-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ Async/await-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá try/catch Promise rejections handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‚úÖ Advanced (Optional)
### _#45._ üü° What is a memory leak and how can you avoid it?

Memory leak ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® JavaScript-‡¶è memory allocated ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ properly released ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá application-‡¶è‡¶∞ performance ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ crash ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Common causes: unused variables, forgotten timers, event listeners, ‡¶¨‡¶æ circular references‡•§  
**Avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º**:  
- `clearTimeout`/`clearInterval` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá timers clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- Event listeners remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ (`removeEventListener`)‡•§  
- Variables null ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ scope ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§  
- WeakMap/WeakSet ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá references manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- Chrome DevTools-‡¶è‡¶∞ Memory tab ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá leaks detect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `element.removeEventListener('click', handler);` unused listeners clean ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#46._ üü° What is tail call optimization?

Tail call optimization (TCO) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript engine-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø optimization technique ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá recursive function calls stack overflow ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á efficient ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø function-‡¶è‡¶∞ last operation ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (tail position), ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® stack frame create ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá existing frame reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
function factorial(n, acc = 1) {
  if (n <= 1) return acc;
  return factorial(n - 1, n * acc); // Tail call
}
```
ES6 TCO support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ V8 engine-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø fully implemented ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ TCO recursion-heavy code-‡¶è memory usage ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#47._ üü° What is a module and how does import/export work?

Module ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ reusable code unit ‡¶Ø‡¶æ variables, functions, ‡¶¨‡¶æ classes encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ES6 modules (`import`/`export`) code organization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependency management ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Export**: `export` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá module-‡¶è‡¶∞ content share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
  ```javascript
  // math.js
  export const add = (a, b) => a + b;
  export default function multiply(a, b) { return a * b; }
  ```
- **Import**: `import` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá module-‡¶è‡¶∞ content use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
  ```javascript
  // main.js
  import { add } from './math.js';
  import multiply from './math.js';
  console.log(add(2, 3)); // 5
  console.log(multiply(2, 3)); // 6
  ```
Modules strict mode-‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser/server-‡¶è `<script type="module">` ‡¶¨‡¶æ Node.js-‡¶è `.mjs` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `package.json` (`"type": "module"`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#48._ üü° What is the purpose of 'typeof' operator?

`typeof` operator ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø unary operator ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã value ‡¶¨‡¶æ variable-‡¶è‡¶∞ data type return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø type checking-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Return values: `"undefined"`, `"number"`, `"string"`, `"boolean"`, `"object"`, `"function"`, `"symbol"`, `"bigint"`‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```javascript
console.log(typeof 42); // "number"
console.log(typeof 'hello'); // "string"
console.log(typeof null); // "object" (historical bug)
console.log(typeof undefined); // "undefined"
```
Limitations: `null`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `"object"` return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç array/object distinction ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á `Array.isArray()` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `instanceof` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

# ‚ú® TypeScript based interview questions
‚úÖ 1. Basics of TypeScript
### _#01._ üîµ What is TypeScript and how is it different from JavaScript?

TypeScript ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø open-source programming language ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ superset‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript-‡¶è static typing ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç advanced features ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ TypeScript code compile ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá JavaScript-‡¶è convert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ browser ‡¶¨‡¶æ Node.js-‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§  
**Differences**:  
- **Typing**: TypeScript static types (e.g., `let x: number = 5`) ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, JavaScript dynamic typing ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Features**: TypeScript-‡¶è interfaces, enums, generics ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript-‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§  
- **Error Checking**: TypeScript compile time-‡¶è type errors ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá, JavaScript runtime-‡¶è‡•§  
- **Tooling**: TypeScript better IDE support ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç autocomplete ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function add(a: number, b: number): number { return a + b; }` TypeScript-‡¶è type-safe, JavaScript-‡¶è `function add(a, b) { return a + b; }`‡•§

### _#02._ üîµ What are the benefits of using TypeScript?

TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ benefits:  
- **Static Typing**: Type errors compile time-‡¶è ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá, runtime bugs ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
- **Better Tooling**: Autocomplete, refactoring, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç IntelliSense support‡•§  
- **Code Maintainability**: Interfaces, types, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modules code organization ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Scalability**: Large codebases-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ideal, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® enterprise applications‡•§  
- **Interoperability**: JavaScript libraries seamlessly ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
- **Early Error Detection**: Code quality ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `let x: string = 123;` error ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: TypeScript-‡¶è `interface User { name: string; age: number; }` type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#03._ üîµ How do you compile TypeScript code to JavaScript?

TypeScript code JavaScript-‡¶è compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá TypeScript compiler (`tsc`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Steps:  
1. **Install TypeScript**: `npm install -g typescript`  
2. **Write TypeScript Code**: `.ts` file-‡¶è code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `example.ts`‡•§  
3. **Compile**: Command line-‡¶è `tsc example.ts` run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `example.js` generate ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
4. **Run JavaScript**: `node example.js` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
**Options**: `tsconfig.json` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá compiler options (e.g., target, module) configure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `tsc --target es6 example.ts` ES6-compatible JavaScript generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Watch mode (`tsc --watch`) auto-compilation ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#04._ üîµ What is tsconfig.json and why is it important?

`tsconfig.json` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript project-‡¶è‡¶∞ configuration file ‡¶Ø‡¶æ compiler options ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç project settings define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø project root-‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  
**Key Properties**:  
- `compilerOptions`: `target` (e.g., ES6), `module` (e.g., CommonJS), `strict` (type checking), `outDir` (output directory)‡•§  
- `include`: Compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ files/folders (e.g., `["src/**/*"]`)‡•§  
- `exclude`: Ignored files (e.g., `["node_modules"]`)‡•§  
**Importance**:  
- Consistent compilation settings ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- Multiple developers-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø project setup ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- IDE integration ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç automation (e.g., `tsc --watch`) ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```json
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "target": "es6",
    "module": "commonjs",
    "outDir": "./dist",
    "strict": true
  },
  "include": ["src/**/*"]
}
```

### _#05._ üîµ What are the main differences between ES6 and TypeScript?

ES6 (ECMAScript 2015) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ standard, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ TypeScript ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ superset‡•§ Main differences:  
- **Typing**: TypeScript static types (e.g., `let x: number`) ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ES6 dynamic typing ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Features**: TypeScript-‡¶è interfaces, enums, generics, access modifiers (e.g., `public`, `private`) ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ES6-‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ES6-‡¶è arrow functions, classes, modules ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ TypeScript ‡¶ì inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Compilation**: TypeScript compile ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá JavaScript-‡¶è convert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ES6 ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø browser/Node.js-‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§  
- **Error Checking**: TypeScript compile-time type checking ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ES6 runtime-‡¶è errors ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Tooling**: TypeScript better IDE support ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type inference ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: TypeScript-‡¶è `function greet(name: string): string { return "Hello " + name; }` type-safe, ES6-‡¶è `function greet(name) { return "Hello " + name; }`‡•§

‚úÖ 2. Type System
### _#06._ üîµ What is a type in TypeScript?

TypeScript-‡¶è type ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø mechanism ‡¶Ø‡¶æ variables, parameters, ‡¶¨‡¶æ return values-‡¶è‡¶∞ data structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ behavior define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø static type checking ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ compile time-‡¶è errors ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Types built-in (e.g., `number`, `string`) ‡¶¨‡¶æ custom (e.g., interfaces, type aliases) ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let age: number = 30;` ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `number` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã type‡•§ Types code-‡¶è‡¶∞ predictability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#07._ üîµ What are the different built-in types in TypeScript?

TypeScript-‡¶è built-in types:  
- **Primitive Types**: `number`, `string`, `boolean`, `null`, `undefined`, `symbol`, `bigint`‡•§  
- **Object Types**: `object`, `Array`, `Function`, `Date` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§  
- **Special Types**: `any` (any value), `unknown` (type-safe alternative to `any`), `never` (no value), `void` (no return value)‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
let count: number = 10;
let name: string = "John";
let isActive: boolean = true;
let data: any = 42;
```
JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ types TypeScript-‡¶è ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç additional type safety ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#08._ üîµ What is the difference between `any`, `unknown`, and `never`?

- **any**: Type checking disable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã value accept ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Unsafe, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ errors ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x: any = 10; x = "hello";`  
- **unknown**: Type-safe alternative to `any`‡•§ Value-‡¶è‡¶∞ type unknown, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á operations ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá type narrow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x: unknown; if (typeof x === "string") { x.toUpperCase(); }`  
- **never**: ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã value represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Functions ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã return ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (e.g., throws error) ‡¶¨‡¶æ impossible cases-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function error(): never { throw new Error(); }`  
`unknown` safer, `any` risky, `never` specific edge cases-‡¶è‡•§

### _#09._ üîµ What is the difference between `null` and `undefined` in TypeScript?

- **null**: Intentional absence of value‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø variable explicitly `null` assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let x: null = null;`  
- **undefined**: Variable declared ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ value assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let y: undefined;`  
**TypeScript-‡¶è**:  
- `strictNullChecks` enable ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá, `null` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `undefined` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ type ‡¶¨‡¶æ union types-‡¶è assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `let z: number | null = null;`  
- JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã loose equality (`==`) `null` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `undefined`-‡¶ï‡ßá equal ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ strict equality (`===`) ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
TypeScript-‡¶è `strictNullChecks` safer code ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#10._ üîµ What is type inference?

Type inference ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ capability ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá compiler automatically variable-‡¶è‡¶∞ type determine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá explicit type annotation ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø code-‡¶ï‡ßá concise ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
let x = 10; // TypeScript infers x as number
let name = "John"; // Inferred as string
```
Type inference initialization-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º value-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø value assign ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, default-‡¶è `any` ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Best practices: ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá possible, inference-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ rely ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

### _#11._ üîµ What is type assertion in TypeScript?

Type assertion ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è developer-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø way ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá compiler-‡¶ï‡ßá explicitly ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø value-‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø type narrowing-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ Syntax: `as` ‡¶¨‡¶æ angle brackets (`<>`).  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
let value: any = "Hello";
let strLength: number = (value as string).length; // Type assertion
// Or
let strLength2: number = (<string>value).length;
```
Caveat: Assertion type safety guarantee ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ; wrong assertion runtime errors ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `unknown`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá type checking ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§

### _#12._ üîµ What is type alias?

Type alias ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è custom type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø way ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `type` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø complex types reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type Point = { x: number; y: number };
let point: Point = { x: 10, y: 20 };
type ID = string | number;
let userId: ID = "123";
```
Type alias unions, intersections, primitives, ‡¶¨‡¶æ objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ Interface-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º type alias ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø flexible ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### _#13._ üîµ What is a literal type?

Literal type ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è specific value-‡¶ï‡ßá type ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø exact values (e.g., string literals, number literals) define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
let direction: "up" | "down" | "left" | "right";
direction = "up"; // Valid
direction = "diagonal"; // Error
```
Literal types often union types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø type safety ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç specific values enforce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#14._ üîµ What are union and intersection types?

- **Union Type (`|`)**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø variable multiple types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
let value: string | number;
value = "Hello"; // Valid
value = 42; // Valid
```
- **Intersection Type (`&`)**: Multiple types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ properties combine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type A = { a: number };
type B = { b: string };
let ab: A & B = { a: 1, b: "test" };
```
Union flexibility ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, intersection strictness‡•§ Union-‡¶è common operations ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ shared properties-‡¶è limited‡•§

### _#15._ üîµ What is an enum in TypeScript?

Enum ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è named constants-‡¶è‡¶∞ collection define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø way‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø related values-‡¶è‡¶∞ group organize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type safety ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
enum Color {
  Red, // 0
  Green, // 1
  Blue // 2
}
let c: Color = Color.Green;
console.log(c); // 1
```
Enums numeric (default), string, ‡¶¨‡¶æ mixed ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `enum Status { Active = "ACTIVE", Inactive = "INACTIVE" }`‡•§ Enums code readability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainability ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Compile ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá JavaScript object-‡¶è convert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‚úÖ 3. Functions
### _#16._ üîµ How do you define a function with typed parameters and return value?

TypeScript-‡¶è function-‡¶è‡¶∞ parameters ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç return value-‡¶è‡¶∞ types explicitly define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Syntax-‡¶è parameter-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ `:` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç return type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø function signature-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ `:` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function add(a: number, b: number): number {
  return a + b;
}
```
Arrow function-‡¶è:  
```typescript
const multiply: (x: number, y: number) => number = (x, y) => x * y;
```
Return type optional, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ TypeScript type inference ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Void return-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø: `function log(message: string): void { console.log(message); }`‡•§

### _#17._ üîµ What is the difference between optional and default parameters?

- **Optional Parameters**: `?` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá parameter optional ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Value pass ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `undefined` ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
  ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
  ```typescript
  function greet(name: string, greeting?: string): string {
    return `${greeting || 'Hello'}, ${name}`;
  }
  console.log(greet('John')); // Hello, John
  console.log(greet('John', 'Hi')); // Hi, John
  ```
- **Default Parameters**: Parameter-‡¶è default value set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Value ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá default value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
  ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
  ```typescript
  function greet(name: string, greeting: string = 'Hello'): string {
    return `${greeting}, ${name}`;
  }
  console.log(greet('John')); // Hello, John
  console.log(greet('John', 'Hi')); // Hi, John
  ```
**Difference**: Optional parameters `undefined` ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type checking ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®; default parameters-‡¶è value guaranteed ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

### _#18._ üîµ What are rest parameters in TypeScript?

Rest parameters TypeScript-‡¶è variable number of arguments array ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá accept ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `...` syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Rest parameter-‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ array type ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function sum(...numbers: number[]): number {
  return numbers.reduce((acc, curr) => acc + curr, 0);
}
console.log(sum(1, 2, 3)); // 6
console.log(sum(1)); // 1
```
Rest parameters function-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ parameter ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ TypeScript type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `...numbers: string[]` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ strings accept ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### _#19._ üîµ What is a function overload in TypeScript?

Function overload ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á function-‡¶è‡¶∞ multiple signatures define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ technique, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ different parameter types ‡¶¨‡¶æ return types handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Implementation signature ‡¶∏‡¶¨ cases cover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function combine(a: string, b: string): string;
function combine(a: number, b: number): number;
function combine(a: any, b: any): any {
  return a + b;
}
console.log(combine('Hello', 'World')); // HelloWorld
console.log(combine(5, 10)); // 15
```
Overloads compile time-‡¶è type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Implementation signature actual logic ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#20._ üîµ How can you define a function type?

TypeScript-‡¶è function type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá type alias, interface, ‡¶¨‡¶æ inline type ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Function type parameter types ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç return type specify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
- **Type Alias**:  
  ```typescript
  type AddFn = (a: number, b: number) => number;
  const add: AddFn = (a, b) => a + b;
  ```
- **Interface**:  
  ```typescript
  interface GreetFn {
    (name: string): string;
  }
  const greet: GreetFn = (name) => `Hello, ${name}`;
  ```
- **Inline**:  
  ```typescript
  const multiply: (x: number, y: number) => number = (x, y) => x * y;
  ```
Function types reusable signatures ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç callback functions ‡¶¨‡¶æ APIs-‡¶è type safety ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‚úÖ 4. Interfaces & Objects
### _#21._ üîµ What is an interface in TypeScript?

Interface ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ object-‡¶è‡¶∞ shape ‡¶¨‡¶æ structure define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø properties, methods, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ types specify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Interfaces compile-time checking-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript-‡¶è compile ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
  age: number;
}
const user: User = { name: "John", age: 30 };
```
Interfaces classes, functions, ‡¶¨‡¶æ objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ contract ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#22._ üîµ How is an interface different from a type alias?

**Interface** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Type Alias** ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á types define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø:  
- **Syntax**: Interface `interface` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá, type alias `type` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡•§  
  ```typescript
  interface User { name: string; }
  type UserType = { name: string; };
  ```
- **Extensibility**: Interfaces `extends` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º; type aliases `&` (intersection) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá combine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
  ```typescript
  interface Admin extends User { role: string; }
  type AdminType = UserType & { role: string; };
  ```
- **Declaration Merging**: Interfaces same name ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá redeclare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá merge ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º; type aliases ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
  ```typescript
  interface User { id: number; }
  interface User { email: string; } // Merges: { id: number; email: string; }
  ```
- **Flexibility**: Type aliases unions, literals, primitives-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º; interfaces ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ object shapes-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§  
Interfaces object-oriented design-‡¶è, type aliases flexible scenarios-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§

### _#23._ üîµ How do you use optional properties in an interface?

Optional properties interface-‡¶è `?` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ property-‡¶ï‡ßá optional ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Object-‡¶è property ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì error ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
  age?: number; // Optional
}
const user1: User = { name: "John" }; // Valid
const user2: User = { name: "Jane", age: 25 }; // Valid
```
Optional properties flexible data structures-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® API responses ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ field guaranteed ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#24._ üîµ What is readonly property in interfaces?

`readonly` property interface-‡¶è define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶æ property-‡¶ï‡ßá initialize-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ immutable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Value assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ creation-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface User {
  readonly id: number;
  name: string;
}
const user: User = { id: 1, name: "John" };
user.name = "Jane"; // Valid
user.id = 2; // Error: id is readonly
```
`readonly` immutability ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® unique identifiers-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Array-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `ReadonlyArray<T>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#25._ üîµ Can interfaces extend other interfaces?

‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, interfaces TypeScript-‡¶è `extends` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá other interfaces extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø inheritance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç code reuse ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface Person {
  name: string;
}
interface Employee extends Person {
  role: string;
}
const emp: Employee = { name: "John", role: "Developer" };
```
Multiple interfaces extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:  
```typescript
interface A { a: number; }
interface B { b: string; }
interface C extends A, B { c: boolean; }
const obj: C = { a: 1, b: "test", c: true };
```
Extending interfaces object-oriented design-‡¶è hierarchy ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#26._ üîµ How do you define a nested object with types?

TypeScript-‡¶è nested object-‡¶è‡¶∞ types define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá interfaces ‡¶¨‡¶æ type aliases ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Nested properties-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø inner types define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface Address {
  street: string;
  city: string;
}
interface User {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  address: Address;
}
const user: User = {
  name: "John",
  age: 30,
  address: { street: "123 Main St", city: "Dhaka" }
};
```
Alternative (type alias):  
```typescript
type UserType = {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  address: { street: string; city: string };
};
```
Nested objects complex data structures (e.g., API responses) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá type safety ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‚úÖ 5. Classes in TypeScript
### _#27._ üîµ How do you define a class in TypeScript?

TypeScript-‡¶è class define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `class` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ES6 classes-‡¶è‡¶∞ extension‡•§ Class-‡¶è properties, methods, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç constructor ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç TypeScript type annotations ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç access modifiers ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
class Person {
  name: string;
  age: number;

  constructor(name: string, age: number) {
    this.name = name;
    this.age = age;
  }

  greet(): string {
    return `Hello, ${this.name}`;
  }
}

const person = new Person("John", 30);
console.log(person.greet()); // Hello, John
```
Constructor-‡¶è shorthand: `constructor(public name: string)` automatically property declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#28._ üîµ What is the difference between public, private, and protected modifiers?

TypeScript-‡¶è access modifiers class members-‡¶è‡¶∞ visibility control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:  
- **public**: Default modifier‡•§ Property/method ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º accessible‡•§  
  ```typescript
  class Animal {
    public name: string;
    constructor(name: string) { this.name = name; }
  }
  const dog = new Animal("Dog");
  console.log(dog.name); // Accessible
  ```
- **private**: Property/method ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá accessible‡•§  
  ```typescript
  class Animal {
    private secret: string = "Hidden";
    getSecret() { return this.secret; }
  }
  const cat = new Animal();
  console.log(cat.getSecret()); // Hidden
  console.log(cat.secret); // Error: secret is private
  ```
- **protected**: Class ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç derived classes-‡¶è accessible, ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
  ```typescript
  class Animal {
    protected type: string = "Mammal";
  }
  class Dog extends Animal {
    getType() { return this.type; } // Accessible
  }
  const dog = new Dog();
  console.log(dog.type); // Error: type is protected
  ```
**Difference**: `public` ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá open, `private` most restricted, `protected` inheritance-‡¶è limited access ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#29._ üîµ What is `readonly` in a class?

`readonly` modifier class properties-‡¶ï‡ßá immutable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ initialization (constructor ‡¶¨‡¶æ declaration-‡¶è) ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
class User {
  readonly id: number;
  name: string;

  constructor(id: number, name: string) {
    this.id = id;
    this.name = name;
  }

  updateName(newName: string) {
    this.name = newName; // Valid
    this.id = 2; // Error: id is readonly
  }
}

const user = new User(1, "John");
console.log(user.id); // 1
user.id = 2; // Error
```
`readonly` data integrity ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® unique IDs-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Interface-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã class-‡¶è‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#30._ üîµ What is inheritance in TypeScript classes?

Inheritance ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ feature ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class (child) ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class (parent) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `extends` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Child class parent-‡¶è‡¶∞ members access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
class Animal {
  move() {
    console.log("Moving...");
  }
}

class Dog extends Animal {
  bark() {
    console.log("Woof!");
  }
}

const dog = new Dog();
dog.move(); // Moving...
dog.bark(); // Woof!
```
`super` keyword parent class-‡¶è‡¶∞ constructor ‡¶¨‡¶æ methods call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `super.move()`‡•§ Inheritance code reuse ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç hierarchy ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#31._ üîµ What is an abstract class?

Abstract class ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class ‡¶Ø‡¶æ directly instantiate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç blueprint ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `abstract` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç abstract methods (implementation ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ derived classes-‡¶è implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
abstract class Shape {
  abstract calculateArea(): number; // Abstract method

  getDescription(): string {
    return "This is a shape";
  }
}

class Circle extends Shape {
  radius: number;

  constructor(radius: number) {
    super();
    this.radius = radius;
  }

  calculateArea(): number {
    return Math.PI * this.radius ** 2;
  }
}

const circle = new Circle(5);
console.log(circle.calculateArea()); // 78.539...
console.log(circle.getDescription()); // This is a shape
const shape = new Shape(); // Error: Cannot create an instance of an abstract class
```
Abstract classes polymorphism ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç common functionality share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§

‚úÖ 6. Generics
### _#32._ üîµ What are generics in TypeScript?

Generics ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type-safe code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø functions, classes, ‡¶¨‡¶æ interfaces-‡¶è type parameters ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ specific types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá placeholder ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Generics type safety ‡¶¨‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá flexibility ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function identity<T>(value: T): T {
  return value;
}
console.log(identity<number>(42)); // 42
console.log(identity<string>("Hello")); // Hello
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `T` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã generic type parameter‡•§ Generics type duplication ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç code reusability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### _#33._ üîµ Why and when would you use generics?

**Why**:  
- **Type Safety**: Compile-time type checking ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **Reusability**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á logic different types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
- **Avoid `any`**: `any` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ unsafe nature ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§  
- **Maintainability**: Code cleaner ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scalable ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  

**When**:  
- Functions ‡¶¨‡¶æ classes ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® multiple types handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: Collections (arrays, lists)‡•§  
- Reusable components, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® React components‡•§  
- Utility functions ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `map`, `filter`‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: Array utilities-‡¶è `function getFirst<T>(arr: T[]): T` different array types-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#34._ üîµ How do you write a generic function?

Generic function ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá function name-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá `<T>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá type parameter declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `T` parameter types ‡¶¨‡¶æ return type-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function getPair<T, U>(first: T, second: U): [T, U] {
  return [first, second];
}
const pair = getPair<string, number>("Hello", 42);
console.log(pair); // ["Hello", 42]
```
Type inference ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á explicit type optional:  
```typescript
const pair2 = getPair("Hi", true); // Inferred as [string, boolean]
```
Generic functions type-safe ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#35._ üîµ What is a generic constraint?

Generic constraint ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã generic type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ restriction ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® properties ‡¶¨‡¶æ methods ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ `extends` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
interface HasLength {
  length: number;
}
function getLength<T extends HasLength>(item: T): number {
  return item.length;
}
console.log(getLength("Hello")); // 5
console.log(getLength([1, 2, 3])); // 3
console.log(getLength(42)); // Error: number has no length
```
Constraint type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç invalid operations ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Common constraints: `extends object`, `extends keyof`, ‡¶¨‡¶æ specific interfaces‡•§

### _#36._ üîµ Can you use multiple generics at once?

‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, TypeScript-‡¶è multiple generic type parameters ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø parameter comma ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá separate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `<T, U>`.  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
function merge<T, U>(obj1: T, obj2: U): T & U {
  return { ...obj1, ...obj2 };
}
const result = merge<{ name: string }, { age: number }>(
  { name: "John" },
  { age: 30 }
);
console.log(result); // { name: "John", age: 30 }
```
Multiple generics complex scenarios handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® different types-‡¶è‡¶∞ objects merge ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ Type inference ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:  
```typescript
const result2 = merge({ x: 1 }, { y: "test" }); // Inferred as { x: number } & { y: string }
```

‚úÖ 7. Advanced Types
### _#37._ üîµ What are mapped types in TypeScript?

Mapped types ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ existing type-‡¶è‡¶∞ properties-‡¶ï‡ßá transform ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® type ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø object types-‡¶è‡¶∞ keys iterate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® structure generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Syntax: `{ [K in keyof T]: Type }`‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type User = { name: string; age: number };
type ReadonlyUser = { readonly [K in keyof User]: User[K] };
const user: ReadonlyUser = { name: "John", age: 30 };
user.name = "Jane"; // Error: readonly
```
Built-in mapped types: `Partial<T>`, `Required<T>`, `Readonly<T>`, `Pick<T, K>`‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `Partial<User>` ‡¶∏‡¶¨ properties optional ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### _#38._ üîµ What is the `keyof` operator?

`keyof` operator TypeScript-‡¶è type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ property keys-‡¶è‡¶∞ union type return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø object types-‡¶è‡¶∞ keys dynamically access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type User = { name: string; age: number; id: number };
type UserKeys = keyof User; // "name" | "age" | "id"
let key: UserKeys = "name"; // Valid
key = "email"; // Error
```
`keyof` mapped types, index signatures, ‡¶¨‡¶æ type-safe property access-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `function getProp<T, K extends keyof T>(obj: T, key: K): T[K] { return obj[key]; }`‡•§

### _#39._ üîµ What is the `typeof` operator in type context?

TypeScript-‡¶è `typeof` operator type context-‡¶è value-‡¶è‡¶∞ type extract ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ `typeof` (runtime) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø compile-time type inference ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
const user = { name: "John", age: 30 };
type UserType = typeof user; // { name: string; age: number }
const anotherUser: UserType = { name: "Jane", age: 25 };
```
`typeof` variables, functions, ‡¶¨‡¶æ objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ types capture ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá runtime values ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `const fn = (x: number) => x * 2; type FnType = typeof fn;`‡•§

### _#40._ üîµ What is the `infer` keyword in TypeScript?

`infer` keyword TypeScript-‡¶è conditional types-‡¶è type inference ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø generic type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá type extract ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `infer` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `extends` clause-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type ReturnType<T> = T extends (...args: any) => infer R ? R : never;
type Fn = (x: number) => string;
type Result = ReturnType<Fn>; // string
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `infer R` function-‡¶è‡¶∞ return type extract ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `infer` complex type manipulation-‡¶è, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `ReturnType`, `Parameters`, ‡¶¨‡¶æ custom utilities-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§

### _#41._ üîµ What are conditional types?

Conditional types ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è types dynamically resolve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø way, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `T extends U ? X : Y` syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø type constraints-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá type select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type IsString<T> = T extends string ? "Yes" : "No";
type Test1 = IsString<string>; // "Yes"
type Test2 = IsString<number>; // "No"
```
Conditional types generics, `infer`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `keyof`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá advanced type logic ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: Built-in `Exclude<T, U>` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `Extract<T, U>`‡•§ Nested conditional types ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

### _#42._ üîµ What are template literal types?

Template literal types ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è string literal types-‡¶ï‡ßá manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ template literals (`${}`) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø string types dynamically ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
type Greeting = "Hello";
type Name = "John" | "Jane";
type Message = `${Greeting}, ${Name}!`; // "Hello, John!" | "Hello, Jane!"
```
Union types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá:  
```typescript
type Event = `on${"Click" | "Hover"}`; // "onClick" | "onHover"
```
Template literal types API routes, event names, ‡¶¨‡¶æ string patterns type-safe ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§

### _#43._ üîµ What is the `as const` assertion?

`as const` assertion TypeScript-‡¶è literal values-‡¶ï‡ßá mutable ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá immutable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç specific literal types-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø object/array-‡¶ï‡ßá readonly ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç literal types enforce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:  
```typescript
const colors = ["red", "blue"] as const;
type Color = typeof colors[number]; // "red" | "blue"
colors.push("green"); // Error: readonly
```
Without `as const`:  
```typescript
const colors2 = ["red", "blue"]; // string[]
```
`as const` literal types, enums-‡¶è‡¶∞ alternative, ‡¶¨‡¶æ constant values-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§‡•§ Objects-‡¶è:  
```typescript
const config = { size: 10, theme: "dark" } as const;
// { readonly size: 10; readonly theme: "dark" }
```

‚úÖ 8. Utility Types
### _#44._ üîµ **What is `Partial<T>` and how is it used?**

`Partial<T>` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø utility type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø object type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá optional ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ interface ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø mandatory, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã optional ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `Partial<T>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
  age: number;
}

type PartialUser = Partial<User>;

// ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® PartialUser ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
// {
//   name?: string;
//   age?: number;
// }
```
**Use case:** ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ function ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user object-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `Partial<User>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§



### _#45._ üîµ **What is `Required<T>`?**
