`Required<T>` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø utility type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `Partial<T>`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ object type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá mandatory ‡¶¨‡¶æ required ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø optional ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface User {
  name?: string;
  age?: number;
}

type RequiredUser = Required<User>;

// ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® RequiredUser ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
// {
//   name: string;
//   age: number;
// }
```
**Use case:** ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `Required<T>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø missing ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§



### _#46._ üîµ **What is `Readonly<T>`?**

`Readonly<T>` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø utility type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ object type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá read-only ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
  age: number;
}

type ReadonlyUser = Readonly<User>;

const user: ReadonlyUser = { name: "Alice", age: 30 };
// user.name = "Bob"; // Error: Cannot assign to 'name' because it is a read-only property.
```
**Use case:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã object immutable ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `Readonly<T>` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§



### _#47._ üîµ **What is `Pick<T, K>` and `Omit<T, K>`?**

**`Pick<T, K>`:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø utility type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ object type ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ type ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `K` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø key-‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ union type‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  email: string;
}

type UserSubset = Pick<User, "name" | "age">;

// UserSubset ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
// {
//   name: string;
//   age: number;
// }
```

**`Omit<T, K>`:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ `Pick`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® type ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
type UserWithoutEmail = Omit<User, "email">;

// UserWithoutEmail ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
// {
//   name: string;
//   age: number;
// }
```
**Use case:** `Pick` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ `Omit` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø exclude ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§



### _#48._ üîµ **What is `Record<K, T>`?**

`Record<K, T>` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø utility type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ object type ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá key ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá `K` (union type) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø key-‡¶è‡¶∞ value ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá `T` type-‡¶è‡¶∞‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
type Role = "admin" | "user" | "guest";
type Permissions = { canEdit: boolean; canView: boolean };

type RolePermissions = Record<Role, Permissions>;

// RolePermissions ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
// {
//   admin: Permissions;
//   user: Permissions;
//   guest: Permissions;
// }
```
**Use case:** ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ object ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü key-‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü type-‡¶è‡¶∞ value map ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `Record` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§



### _#49._ üîµ **What is `Exclude<T, U>` and `Extract<T, U>`?**

**`Exclude<T, U>`:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ union type `T` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ member ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã `U`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá assignable‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
type MyUnion = "a" | "b" | "c";
type Excluded = Exclude<MyUnion, "a" | "c">;

// Excluded ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá: "b"
```

**`Extract<T, U>`:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ `Exclude`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ `T` union type ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á member-‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã `U`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá assignable‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
type Extracted = Extract<MyUnion, "a" | "c">;

// Extracted ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá: "a" | "c"
```
**Use case:** `Exclude` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã union type ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü member ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ `Extract` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü member ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§

‚úÖ 9. Type Guards & Safety
### _#50._ üîµ **What are type guards in TypeScript?**

Type guards ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ runtime-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable-‡¶è‡¶∞ specific type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ type narrowing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá TypeScript compiler ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® type-‡¶è‡¶∞‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ conditional logic ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
function example(value: string | number) {
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    // ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá value ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ string type
    console.log(value.toUpperCase());
  } else {
    // ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá value ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ number type
    console.log(value.toFixed());
  }
}
```
**Use case:** Type guards ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® union types ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç specific type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá logic ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#51._ üîµ **How do you use `in`, `typeof`, and `instanceof` as type guards?**

TypeScript-‡¶è `in`, `typeof`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `instanceof` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã type guards ‡¶Ø‡¶æ type narrowing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ use case ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **`typeof`:** Primitive types (string, number, boolean, etc.) ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   ```typescript
   function printValue(value: string | number) {
     if (typeof value === "string") {
       console.log(`String: ${value.toUpperCase()}`);
     } else {
       console.log(`Number: ${value.toFixed(2)}`);
     }
   }
   ```

2. **`instanceof`:** Class instances ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã object ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü class-‡¶è‡¶∞ instance ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
   ```typescript
   class Dog { bark() {} }
   class Cat { meow() {} }

   function makeSound(animal: Dog | Cat) {
     if (animal instanceof Dog) {
       animal.bark();
     } else {
       animal.meow();
     }
   }
   ```

3. **`in`:** Object-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã property ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   ```typescript
   interface User { name: string }
   interface Admin { name: string; role: string }

   function displayRole(person: User | Admin) {
     if ("role" in person) {
       console.log(`Role: ${person.role}`);
     } else {
       console.log(`Name: ${person.name}`);
     }
   }
   ```

**Use case:** `typeof` primitive types-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, `instanceof` class-based objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ `in` interface ‡¶¨‡¶æ object property ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§



### _#52._ üîµ **What is a discriminated union and how is it used?**

Discriminated union ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï type-‡¶è‡¶∞ union type ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø type-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø common property ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá (‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ literal type) ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá discriminant ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á discriminant ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ type narrowing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface Circle {
  kind: "circle"; // discriminant
  radius: number;
}

interface Square {
  kind: "square"; // discriminant
  side: number;
}

type Shape = Circle | Square;

function getArea(shape: Shape) {
  switch (shape.kind) {
    case "circle":
      return Math.PI * shape.radius ** 2;
    case "square":
      return shape.side ** 2;
  }
}
```

**How it‚Äôs used:**
- Discriminant property (`kind`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ easily identify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® type-‡¶è‡¶∞ object ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§
- Switch case ‡¶¨‡¶æ if-else ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá type narrowing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ code safe ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type errors ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Discriminated union ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï related types ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ unique identifier ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® shape calculations ‡¶¨‡¶æ API response parsing-‡¶è‡•§

‚úÖ 10. Modules and Tooling
### _#53._ üîµ **How do you import and export modules in TypeScript?**

TypeScript-‡¶è modules import ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç export ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ES Modules-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá TypeScript type safety ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type annotations ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `import` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `export` keywords ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

**Export:**
- **Named Export:** Specific variables, functions, ‡¶¨‡¶æ classes export ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
  ```typescript
  // math.ts
  export const add = (a: number, b: number): number => a + b;
  export interface MathOperation {
    calculate: (x: number, y: number) => number;
  }
  ```
- **Default Export:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø module ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá single default export ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
  ```typescript
  // user.ts
  export default class User {
    constructor(public name: string) {}
  }
  ```

**Import:**
- **Named Import:**
  ```typescript
  // main.ts
  import { add, MathOperation } from './math';

  const op: MathOperation = { calculate: add };
  console.log(add(2, 3)); // 5
  ```
- **Default Import:**
  ```typescript
  import User from './user';

  const user = new User("Alice");
  ```
- **Namespace Import:** ‡¶∏‡¶¨ export ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
  ```typescript
  import * as Math from './math';
  console.log(Math.add(2, 3));
  ```

**Use case:** Modules ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø code organization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusability-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá code ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#54._ üîµ **What is declaration merging?**

Declaration merging ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ multiple declarations (interfaces, namespaces, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá merge ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single definition ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ interfaces ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç namespaces-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example (Interface Merging):**
```typescript
interface User {
  name: string;
}

interface User {
  age: number;
}

// Merged result:
// interface User {
//   name: string;
//   age: number;
// }
```

**Rules:**
- Interface-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá multiple declarations ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá TypeScript ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã automatically merge ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Namespace ‡¶¨‡¶æ module declarations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Declaration merging ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø third-party library-‡¶è‡¶∞ type definitions extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ modular‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá interface define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#55._ üîµ **What is a `.d.ts` file and when do you use it?**

`.d.ts` file ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ declaration file ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ type information ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã implementation (logic) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ JavaScript code ‡¶¨‡¶æ libraries-‡¶è‡¶∞ type definitions ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
// my-lib.d.ts
declare function greet(name: string): string;

// main.ts
import { greet } from './my-lib';
console.log(greet("Alice")); // TypeScript type checking ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ implementation JS ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§
```

**When to use:**
- JavaScript libraries (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Lodash, jQuery) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
- Project-‡¶è‡¶∞ global type definitions declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
- TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø external modules-‡¶è‡¶∞ types ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® DefinitelyTyped ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `@types` packages‡•§

**Use case:** `.d.ts` files ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ JavaScript code-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ type checking integrate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§



### _#56._ üîµ **What are ambient declarations in TypeScript?**

Ambient declarations ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® declarations ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ type information ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã runtime implementation ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ `.d.ts` files-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶æ `declare` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ external JavaScript code ‡¶¨‡¶æ global variables-‡¶è‡¶∞ types define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
// ambient.d.ts
declare const MY_GLOBAL: string;

declare module "my-lib" {
  export function myFunction(): void;
}
```

**Key Points:**
- `declare` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ambient declarations-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã runtime-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã code generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ global variables, third-party libraries, ‡¶¨‡¶æ browser APIs (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `window`, `document`) describe ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Ambient declarations ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ JavaScript libraries ‡¶¨‡¶æ global objects-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø type safety ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ implementation ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ control-‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§


‚úÖ 11. React with TypeScript (Bonus if using React)
### _#57._ üîµ **How do you type props and state in a React component?**

TypeScript-‡¶è React component-‡¶è‡¶∞ props ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ interface ‡¶¨‡¶æ type ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Functional components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç class components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§

**Functional Component (Props):**
```typescript
interface MyComponentProps {
  name: string;
  age?: number; // Optional prop
}

const MyComponent: React.FC<MyComponentProps> = ({ name, age }) => {
  return <div>Hello, {name}! Age: {age ?? "N/A"}</div>;
};
```

**State in Functional Component (useState):**
```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';

interface UserState {
  name: string;
  isActive: boolean;
}

const MyComponent = () => {
  const [user, setUser] = useState<UserState>({ name: "Alice", isActive: true });

  return <div>{user.name}</div>;
};
```

**Class Component (Props and State):**
```typescript
interface MyComponentProps {
  title: string;
}

interface MyComponentState {
  count: number;
}

class MyComponent extends React.Component<MyComponentProps, MyComponentState> {
  state: MyComponentState = { count: 0 };

  render() {
    return <div>{this.props.title}: {this.state.count}</div>;
  }
}
```

**Use case:** Props ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ensure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá component-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type errors ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§



### _#58._ üîµ **What is `FC` (FunctionComponent) and when should you use it?**

`React.FC` (FunctionComponent) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø built-in type ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional React components-‡¶è‡¶∞ type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ props-‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç children prop ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```typescript
interface MyComponentProps {
  message: string;
}

const MyComponent: React.FC<MyComponentProps> = ({ message, children }) => {
  return (
    <div>
      {message}
      {children} {/* children automatically typed */}
    </div>
  );
};
```

**When to use:**
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø functional component ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props-‡¶è‡¶∞ type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® component children accept ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ `FC` ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá `children` prop ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Simple components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá complex type logic ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

**When not to use:**
- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø component-‡¶è generic types ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex return types ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `FC` ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø function type define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§
  ```typescript
  function GenericComponent<T>({ data }: { data: T }) {
    return <div>{String(data)}</div>;
  }
  ```

**Use case:** `FC` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø straightforward functional components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø type safety ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#59._ üîµ **How do you type event handlers like `onChange`, `onSubmit`?**

TypeScript-‡¶è React event handlers (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `onChange`, `onSubmit`) ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ React-‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in event types ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `React.ChangeEvent` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `React.FormEvent`‡•§

**Typing `onChange` (Input):**
```typescript
interface FormProps {
  value: string;
  onChange: (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => void;
}

const MyInput: React.FC<FormProps> = ({ value, onChange }) => {
  return <input value={value} onChange={onChange} />;
};

// Usage
const App = () => {
  const [value, setValue] = useState("");
  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setValue(e.target.value);
  };

  return <MyInput value={value} onChange={handleChange} />;
};
```

**Typing `onSubmit` (Form):**
```typescript
const MyForm: React.FC = () => {
  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    console.log("Form submitted");
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
};
```

**Common Event Types:**
- `React.ChangeEvent<T>`: Input, select, textarea-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- `React.FormEvent<T>`: Form submission-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- `React.MouseEvent<T>`: Click, hover ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
- `React.KeyboardEvent<T>`: Key press-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

**Use case:** Event handlers ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ensure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá event object-‡¶è‡¶∞ properties (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `e.target.value`) ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§



### _#60._ üîµ **How do you type `useState`, `useEffect`, and `useRef` in TypeScript?**

TypeScript-‡¶è React hooks ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `useState`, `useEffect`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `useRef` ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶æ, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ React-‡¶è‡¶∞ types ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Typing `useState`:**
```typescript
import { useState } from 'react';

const MyComponent = () => {
  // Simple type
  const [count, setCount] = useState<number>(0);

  // Complex type
  interface User {
    name: string;
    age: number;
  }
  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);

  return <div>{user?.name ?? count}</div>;
};
```

**Typing `useEffect`:**
`useEffect` ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ type annotation ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ void ‡¶¨‡¶æ cleanup function return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá dependencies-‡¶è‡¶∞ types ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
```typescript
import { useEffect } from 'react';

const MyComponent = ({ id }: { id: number }) => {
  useEffect(() => {
    console.log(`ID changed: ${id}`);
    return () => console.log("Cleanup");
  }, [id]); // id: number

  return <div>ID: {id}</div>;
};
```

**Typing `useRef`:**
`useRef` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: DOM elements ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç mutable values-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
```typescript
import { useRef } from 'react';

const MyComponent = () => {
  // DOM element ref
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  // Mutable value ref
  const countRef = useRef<number>(0);

  const focusInput = () => {
    inputRef.current?.focus();
    countRef.current += 1;
  };

  return <input ref={inputRef} onClick={focusInput} />;
};
```

**Key Points:**
- `useState`: Generic type ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá state-‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø (`useState<T>`).
- `useEffect`: Dependencies-‡¶è‡¶∞ types ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, cleanup function optional.
- `useRef`: Generic type ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ref-‡¶è‡¶∞ initial value ‡¶¨‡¶æ DOM element ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø (`useRef<T>`).

**Use case:** Hooks ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ensure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá state, effects, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç refs ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç type errors ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§


# ‚ú® React based interview questions
‚úÖ 1. Basics & Introduction
### _#01._ üü£ **What is ReactJS and why is it used?**

ReactJS ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø open-source JavaScript library ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Facebook ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ develop ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ user interface (UI) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá single-page applications (SPAs)-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ component-based architecture follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI-‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modular ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Why used:**
- **Fast Rendering:** Virtual DOM ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá React UI updates ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Reusable Components:** Code reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ development ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Large Ecosystem:** React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Redux, React Router ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø libraries integrate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§
- **Community Support:** ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º community ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç resources ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ learning ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç problem-solving ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Flexibility:** React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ UI layer-‡¶è focus ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á backend ‡¶¨‡¶æ state management-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã tech ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#02._ üü£ **What are the main features of React?**

React-‡¶è‡¶∞ main features ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Component-Based Architecture:** UI-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü reusable components-‡¶è ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Virtual DOM:** Real DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ lightweight copy, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ updates efficient ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **JSX:** JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML-like syntax, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Unidirectional Data Flow:** Data parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child components-‡¶è flow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ state management predictable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **React Hooks:** Functional components-‡¶è state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle features ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `useState`, `useEffect`)‡•§
- **Declarative UI:** Code-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ describe ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, React ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Cross-Platform:** React Native-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá mobile apps develop ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#03._ üü£ **What is the difference between React and other frontend frameworks (e.g., Angular or Vue)?**

| **Aspect**            | **React**                                                                 | **Angular**                                                              | **Vue**                                                                 |
|-----------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Type**              | Library (‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ UI layer)                                                  | Full-fledged Framework                                                  | Progressive Framework                                                   |
| **Learning Curve**    | Relatively easy, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ React ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º                                    | Steep, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Angular-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá TypeScript, RxJS ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º           | Moderate, React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Angular-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá lightweight         |
| **Data Binding**      | Unidirectional (one-way)                                                  | Two-way binding                                                         | Two-way binding (optional)                                               |
| **DOM Manipulation**  | Virtual DOM                                                              | Real DOM                                                                | Virtual DOM                                                             |
| **Structure**         | Flexible, developer ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá state management (Redux) ‡¶¨‡¶æ routing choose ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá | Opinionated, built-in solutions (routing, forms, etc.)                  | Flexible, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ built-in solutions ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá                                 |
| **Ecosystem**         | Third-party libraries ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ (React Router, Redux)                        | Built-in tools (Angular CLI, Material)                                  | Built-in + third-party (Vuex, Vue Router)                                |
| **Use Case**          | Dynamic, component-heavy UIs                                             | Large-scale, enterprise apps                                            | Small to medium apps, gradual adoption ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨                           |

**Summary:** React flexibility ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lightweight nature-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø popular, Angular enterprise apps-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Vue ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ø‡•§



### _#04._ üü£ **What is JSX and why is it used?**

JSX (JavaScript XML) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø syntax extension ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML-like code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá UI structure combine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Why used:**
- **Readable Code:** JSX-‡¶è‡¶∞ syntax HTML-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á UI ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ intuitive ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **JavaScript Integration:** JSX-‡¶è JavaScript expressions (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `{variable}`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Type Safety:** TypeScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá JSX ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Compiled to JS:** Babel JSX-‡¶ï‡ßá `React.createElement` calls-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø optimized‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const element = <h1>Hello, {name}!</h1>;
// Compiles to:
const element = React.createElement("h1", null, "Hello, ", name, "!");
```

**Use case:** JSX UI components ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ developer experience ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§



### _#05._ üü£ **What are components in React?**

Components ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ building blocks, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü reusable ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã independent ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable code snippets ‡¶Ø‡¶æ specific functionality ‡¶¨‡¶æ UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Types:**
- **Functional Components:** Simple functions ‡¶Ø‡¶æ props ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá JSX return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  ```jsx
  const MyComponent = ({ name }: { name: string }) => <div>Hello, {name}</div>;
  ```
- **Class Components:** Class-based, state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  ```jsx
  class MyComponent extends React.Component<{ name: string }> {
    render() {
      return <div>Hello, {this.props.name}</div>;
    }
  }
  ```

**Features:**
- Props ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá dynamic data render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- State ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá internal data manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Nested components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá complex UI build ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø UI-‡¶ï‡ßá modular ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#06._ üü£ **What is the difference between functional and class components?**

| **Aspect**              | **Functional Components**                                      | **Class Components**                                         |
|-------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Syntax**              | Simple function, JSX return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                              | Class extends `React.Component`, `render` method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá |
| **State Management**    | `useState` hook ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá state manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                       | `this.state` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setState` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá state manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá          |
| **Lifecycle Methods**   | `useEffect` hook ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá lifecycle handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                  | Built-in lifecycle methods (e.g., `componentDidMount`)       |
| **Readability**         | Concise ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç less boilerplate                                  | More boilerplate (class, `this` binding)                    |
| **Performance**         | Slightly better, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ simpler structure                      | Slightly heavier, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ class overhead                       |
| **Usage**               | Modern React-‡¶è preferred (hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø)                     | Legacy code ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex lifecycle ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá                 |

**Example (Functional):**
```jsx
const Counter = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
  return <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>{count}</button>;
};
```

**Example (Class):**
```jsx
class Counter extends React.Component {
  state = { count: 0 };
  render() {
    return <button onClick={() => this.setState({ count: this.state.count + 1 })}>{this.state.count}</button>;
  }
}
```

**Use case:** Functional components modern React-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Class components legacy code-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶æ specific use case-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#07._ üü£ **What is a single-page application (SPA)?**

Single-Page Application (SPA) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø web application ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single HTML page ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamically content update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page reload ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React SPA build ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø popular‡•§

**Key Features:**
- **Client-Side Rendering:** JavaScript (React) browser-‡¶è UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Routing:** React Router-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã libraries ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page navigation handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Fast Experience:** Page reload ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ content update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á user experience smooth‡•§
- **API Integration:** Backend ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® REST ‡¶¨‡¶æ GraphQL)‡•§

**Example:** Gmail, Facebook-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã apps SPA, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá navigation page refresh ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** SPA ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø fast, interactive web apps ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user experience priority‡•§



### _#08._ üü£ **What is the role of Babel and Webpack in React?**

**Babel:**
- Babel ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript compiler ‡¶Ø‡¶æ modern JavaScript (ES6+) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JSX-‡¶ï‡ßá browser-compatible JavaScript-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Role in React:**
  - JSX-‡¶ï‡ßá `React.createElement` calls-‡¶è transform ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - ES6+ features (arrow functions, destructuring) ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã browsers-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø polyfill ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Example: `<div>Hello</div>` ‚Üí `React.createElement("div", null, "Hello")`.

**Webpack:**
- Webpack ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø module bundler ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript, CSS, images ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø assets-‡¶ï‡ßá bundle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá production-ready files ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Role in React:**
  - Modules (JS/TS files) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependencies ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single bundle-‡¶è combine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Code splitting, minification, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç tree-shaking ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá performance optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Loaders (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® babel-loader, ts-loader) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá TypeScript/JSX process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Dev server (hot reloading) provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá development-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

**Use case:** Babel React-‡¶è‡¶∞ modern syntax support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Webpack assets bundle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá app-‡¶ï‡ßá fast ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç production-ready ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§


‚úÖ 2. Props & State
### _#09._ üü£ **What is props in React?**

Props (properties) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component-‡¶è‡¶∞ input, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component-‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Props read-only, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé child component-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const Greeting = ({ name }) => <h1>Hello, {name}!</h1>;

// Parent component
const App = () => <Greeting name="Alice" />;
```

**Key Points:**
- Props ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã object ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component-‡¶è‡¶∞ attributes ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Functions, objects, arrays, ‡¶¨‡¶æ primitive values ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá props ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Props immutable, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á child component ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ read ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child-‡¶è data ‡¶¨‡¶æ behavior (callbacks) ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#10._ üü£ **What is the difference between props and state?**

| **Aspect**         | **Props**                                                                 | **State**                                                                |
|--------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Definition**     | Parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component-‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã data                                | Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                |
| **Mutability**     | Immutable (read-only)                                                     | Mutable (component-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º)                            |
| **Source**         | Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá                                                | Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (useState ‡¶¨‡¶æ this.state)              |
| **Usage**          | Data passing ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç communication-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø                                   | Dynamic UI updates (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® form input, counter)                           |
| **Example**        | `<Button label="Click" />`                                               | `const [count, setCount] = useState(0);`                                |

**Example:**
```jsx
const Counter = ({ initialValue }) => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(initialValue); // State
  return <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>{count}</button>;
};

// Parent
const App = () => <Counter initialValue={0} />; // Props
```

**Use case:** Props data passing-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, state internal changes manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§



### _#11._ üü£ **What is state lifting in React?**

State lifting (lifting state up) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá state ‡¶ï‡ßá child components ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ common parent component-‡¶è move ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá multiple components state share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const Parent = () => {
  const [value, setValue] = useState("");

  return (
    <>
      <Child1 value={value} onChange={setValue} />
      <Child2 value={value} />
    </>
  );
};

const Child1 = ({ value, onChange }) => (
  <input value={value} onChange={(e) => onChange(e.target.value)} />
);

const Child2 = ({ value }) => <p>Value: {value}</p>;
```

**How it works:**
- State (`value`) parent-‡¶è define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Child components props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update function ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ sibling components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data sharing enable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** State lifting ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® multiple components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá shared state ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® form data ‡¶¨‡¶æ user input‡•§



### _#12._ üü£ **What is the difference between controlled and uncontrolled components?**

| **Aspect**              | **Controlled Components**                                           | **Uncontrolled Components**                                       |
|-------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Definition**          | State ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá input-‡¶è‡¶∞ value control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º                         | DOM ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá input-‡¶è‡¶∞ value manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                              |
| **State Management**    | Component state-‡¶è value store ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, props ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá update     | Value DOM-‡¶è store ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ref ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º                  |
| **Example**             | `<input value={state} onChange={handleChange} />`                 | `<input ref={inputRef} />`                                      |
| **Control**             | React fully controls input                                        | DOM controls input, React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                      |
| **Use Case**            | Form validation, dynamic updates                                  | Simple forms, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá state management ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á                 |

**Controlled Component Example:**
```jsx
const ControlledInput = () => {
  const [value, setValue] = useState("");
  return <input value={value} onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)} />;
};
```

**Uncontrolled Component Example:**
```jsx
const UncontrolledInput = () => {
  const inputRef = useRef(null);
  const handleSubmit = () => console.log(inputRef.current.value);
  return <input ref={inputRef} />;
};
```

**Use case:** Controlled components complex forms-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, uncontrolled components simple cases-‡¶è‡•§



### _#13._ üü£ **What is prop drilling, and how do you avoid it?**

**Prop drilling** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá props ‡¶ï‡ßá multiple nested components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá‡¶∞ components-‡¶è props-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ code complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const App = () => {
  const data = "Hello";
  return <Parent data={data} />;
};

const Parent = ({ data }) => <Child data={data} />; // data-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
const Child = ({ data }) => <GrandChild data={data} />; // data-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
const GrandChild = ({ data }) => <div>{data}</div>;
```

**How to avoid:**
1. **React Context API:**
   ```jsx
   const DataContext = createContext(null);

   const App = () => (
     <DataContext.Provider value="Hello">
       <GrandChild />
     </DataContext.Provider>
   );

   const GrandChild = () => {
     const data = useContext(DataContext);
     return <div>{data}</div>;
   };
   ```
2. **State Management Libraries:** Redux, Zustand, ‡¶¨‡¶æ Recoil ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá global state manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
3. **Component Composition:** Props-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá children ‡¶¨‡¶æ render props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
   ```jsx
   const Parent = ({ children }) => <div>{children}</div>;
   ```

**Use case:** Prop drilling avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Context ‡¶¨‡¶æ state management ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø large-scale apps-‡¶è‡•§



### _#14._ üü£ **What is the use of the key prop in a list?**

`key` prop ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø special attribute ‡¶Ø‡¶æ list-‡¶è‡¶∞ items (elements) uniquely identify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ React-‡¶ï‡ßá efficient rendering ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Why needed:**
- React Virtual DOM-‡¶è changes track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `key` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- List items add, remove, ‡¶¨‡¶æ reorder ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá React ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® item ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Without `key`, React entire list re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ performance issue ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const List = ({ items }) => (
  <ul>
    {items.map((item) => (
      <li key={item.id}>{item.name}</li> // key ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá unique id
    ))}
  </ul>
);
```

**Rules:**
- `key` unique ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá list-‡¶è‡¶∞ sibling elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§
- Index ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ list order change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá issue ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Stable IDs (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® database ID) best choice‡•§

**Use case:** `key` prop ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø lists efficiently render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unnecessary re-renders ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


‚úÖ 3. Hooks
### _#15._ üü£ **What is a hook in React?**

React-‡¶è Hook ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã special functions ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional components-‡¶è state, lifecycle features, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø React functionalities ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Hooks React 16.8-‡¶è introduce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá class components ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á complex logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:** `useState`, `useEffect`, `useContext` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
**Use case:** Hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø functional components-‡¶è state management, side effects, ‡¶¨‡¶æ context access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#16._ üü£ **What is useState and how does it work?**

`useState` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional components-‡¶è state manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state variable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useState` initial value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá state initialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- State update ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useState } from 'react';

const Counter = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0); // Initial state: 0
  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {count}</p>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>Increment</button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**Use case:** `useState` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø simple state (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® counter, form input) manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#17._ üü£ **What is useEffect and how does it work?**

`useEffect` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ side effects (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® data fetching, DOM manipulation, subscriptions) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ component lifecycle methods-‡¶è‡¶∞ (mount, update, unmount) ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useEffect` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø callback function ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component render-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Dependency array ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® effect run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- Cleanup function return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá unmount ‡¶¨‡¶æ re-run ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá cleanup ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

const DataFetcher = () => {
  const [data, setData] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('https://api.example.com/data')
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then(setData);
    return () => console.log('Cleanup'); // Cleanup on unmount
  }, []); // Empty dependency array: runs once on mount

  return <div>{data ? data.name : 'Loading...'}</div>;
};
```

**Use case:** `useEffect` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø API calls, timers, ‡¶¨‡¶æ event listeners setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#18._ üü£ **What are the rules of hooks?**

React hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® rules ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ESLint plugin (`eslint-plugin-react-hooks`) enforce ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

1. **Only call hooks at the top level:**
   - Hooks ‡¶ï‡ßá loops, conditions, ‡¶¨‡¶æ nested functions-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
   - ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º component-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ custom hook-‡¶è‡¶∞ top level-‡¶è call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
   - **Reason:** Hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ call order consistent ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø render-‡¶è‡•§

2. **Only call hooks from React function components or custom hooks:**
   - Hooks ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ functional components ‡¶¨‡¶æ custom hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
   - Regular JavaScript functions ‡¶¨‡¶æ class components-‡¶è hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
   - **Reason:** Hooks React-‡¶è‡¶∞ internal state management-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá tied‡•§

**Example (Correct):**
```jsx
const MyComponent = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0); // Top level
  useEffect(() => {}, []);
  return <div>{count}</div>;
};
```

**Example (Incorrect):**
```jsx
const MyComponent = () => {
  if (true) {
    const [count, setCount] = useState(0); // Error: Not top level
  }
  return <div></div>;
};
```

**Use case:** Rules follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá hooks predictable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç bug-free ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§



### _#19._ üü£ **What is useRef and how is it used?**

`useRef` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ mutable reference object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component-‡¶è‡¶∞ lifetime ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá persist ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ DOM elements access ‡¶¨‡¶æ mutable values store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useRef` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `{ current: initialValue }` object return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `current` property change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

**Example (DOM Access):**
```jsx
import { useRef } from 'react';

const MyInput = () => {
  const inputRef = useRef(null);

  const focusInput = () => {
    inputRef.current.focus(); // DOM element access
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <input ref={inputRef} />
      <button onClick={focusInput}>Focus</button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**Example (Mutable Value):**
```jsx
const Counter = () => {
  const countRef = useRef(0);

  const increment = () => {
    countRef.current += 1; // No re-render
    console.log(countRef.current);
  };

  return <button onClick={increment}>Increment</button>;
};
```

**Use case:** `useRef` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM manipulation, timers, ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ mutable values track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#20._ üü£ **What is useMemo and why would you use it?**

`useMemo` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ expensive calculations memoize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá unnecessary re-computations ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø value return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useMemo` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø callback function ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependency array ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Dependencies unchanged ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá memoized value return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useMemo } from 'react';

const ExpensiveComponent = ({ numbers }) => {
  const sum = useMemo(() => {
    console.log('Calculating sum...');
    return numbers.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  }, [numbers]); // Recompute only if numbers change

  return <div>Sum: {sum}</div>;
};
```

**Why use:**
- Performance optimization-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® complex calculations (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® sorting, filtering) render-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ run ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Unnecessary re-renders prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** `useMemo` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø large datasets process ‡¶¨‡¶æ computationally heavy operations optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#21._ üü£ **What is useCallback?**

`useCallback` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ memoized callback function return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá function unnecessary re-creation ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useCallback` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø callback function ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependency array ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Dependencies unchanged ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá same function reference return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useCallback, useState } from 'react';

const Button = ({ onClick }) => {
  console.log('Button re-rendered');
  return <button onClick={onClick}>Click</button>;
};

const App = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  const handleClick = useCallback(() => {
    setCount(count + 1);
  }, [count]); // Same function unless count changes

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {count}</p>
      <Button onClick={handleClick} />
    </div>
  );
};
```

**Why use:**
- Child components-‡¶è function props ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º unnecessary re-renders prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
- Performance optimization-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

**Use case:** `useCallback` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® functions child components-‡¶è props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç re-render avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#22._ üü£ **What is useContext and how does it work?**

`useContext` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Context API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, prop drilling ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡•§ Context global state ‡¶¨‡¶æ shared data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**How it works:**
- `createContext` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `Provider` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá context value set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `useContext` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá component-‡¶è value access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { createContext, useContext, useState } from 'react';

const ThemeContext = createContext(null);

const App = () => {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState('light');

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme }}>
      <Child />
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};

const Child = () => {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useContext(ThemeContext);
  return (
    <div>
      <p>Theme: {theme}</p>
      <button onClick={() => setTheme('dark')}>Toggle Theme</button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**Use case:** `useContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø theme, user data, ‡¶¨‡¶æ app-wide settings share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#23._ üü£ **What is useReducer and how is it different from useState?**

`useReducer` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ complex state logic manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Redux-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã reducer pattern follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- `useReducer` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reducer function ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç initial state ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `dispatch` function ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá actions trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Reducer state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useReducer } from 'react';

const initialState = { count: 0 };

const reducer = (state, action) => {
  switch (action.type) {
    case 'increment':
      return { count: state.count + 1 };
    case 'decrement':
      return { count: state.count - 1 };
    default:
      return state;
  }
};

const Counter = () => {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(reducer, initialState);

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {state.count}</p>
      <button onClick={() => dispatch({ type: 'increment' })}>Increment</button>
      <button onClick={() => dispatch({ type: 'decrement' })}>Decrement</button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**Difference from useState:**

| **Aspect**          | **useState**                                     | **useReducer**                                  |
|---------------------|-------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| **Purpose**         | Simple state management                         | Complex state logic                            |
| **API**             | `[state, setState]`                             | `[state, dispatch]`                            |
| **Logic**           | Direct state updates                            | Reducer function ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá state updates           |
| **Use Case**        | Single value ‡¶¨‡¶æ simple objects                  | Multiple related states ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex transitions |
| **Example**         | Form input, toggle                              | Form with multiple fields, state machines      |

**Use case:** `useReducer` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® state transitions complex ‡¶¨‡¶æ multiple related states manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§


### _#24._ üü£ **What is a custom hook?**

Custom hook ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø user-defined React hook, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ reusable logic encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ `use` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç built-in hooks (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `useState`, `useEffect`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá logic ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const useWindowSize = () => {
  const [windowSize, setWindowSize] = useState({
    width: window.innerWidth,
    height: window.innerHeight,
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleResize = () => {
      setWindowSize({ width: window.innerWidth, height: window.innerHeight });
    };
    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
  }, []);

  return windowSize;
};

// Usage
const MyComponent = () => {
  const { width, height } = useWindowSize();
  return <div>Window: {width} x {height}</div>;
};
```

**Key Points:**
- Custom hooks reusable logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ rules (top level, only in components/hooks) follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ UI logic ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá separate ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Custom hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø API fetching, form handling, ‡¶¨‡¶æ reusable behaviors (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® window size tracking) implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


‚úÖ 4. Advanced Hooks & Concepts
### _#25._ üü£ **What is the difference between a custom hook and a higher-order component (HOC)?**

| **Aspect**              | **Custom Hook**                                              | **Higher-Order Component (HOC)**                             |
|-------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Definition**          | JavaScript function ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá reusable logic encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ | Function ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá enhanced component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **Usage**               | Functional components-‡¶è logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§                   | Components-‡¶è props ‡¶¨‡¶æ behavior inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§                |
| **Syntax**              | `use` prefix ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£, hooks rules follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§          | Regular function ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                    |
| **Example**             | `useWindowSize` hook window size track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                | `withAuth` HOC authentication logic ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§               |
| **Code Sharing**        | Logic ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ functional components ‡¶¨‡¶æ hooks-‡¶è share ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§      | Logic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI behavior class/functional components-‡¶è share ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ |
| **Flexibility**         | Hooks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá modern React-‡¶è preferred‡•§                    | Legacy code-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§, ‡¶ï‡¶Æ flexible‡•§                  |

**Example (Custom Hook):**
```jsx
const useToggle = () => {
  const [isOn, setIsOn] = useState(false);
  return [isOn, () => setIsOn(!isOn)];
};

const MyComponent = () => {
  const [isOn, toggle] = useToggle();
  return <button onClick={toggle}>{isOn ? 'On' : 'Off'}</button>;
};
```

**Example (HOC):**
```jsx
const withLogger = (WrappedComponent) => {
  return (props) => {
    console.log('Rendering', WrappedComponent.name);
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
};

const MyComponent = ({ name }) => <div>{name}</div>;
const EnhancedComponent = withLogger(MyComponent);
```

**Use case:** Custom hooks modern React-‡¶è logic reuse-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, HOCs legacy code ‡¶¨‡¶æ cross-cutting concerns (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® logging, auth) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#26._ üü£ **What is a higher-order component (HOC)?**

Higher-Order Component (HOC) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø pattern ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ HOCs code reuse ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logic sharing-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const withAuth = (WrappedComponent) => {
  return (props) => {
    const isAuthenticated = checkAuth(); // Assume some auth check
    return isAuthenticated ? <WrappedComponent {...props} /> : <div>Login required</div>;
  };
};

const Profile = ({ user }) => <div>{user.name}</div>;
const AuthProfile = withAuth(Profile);
```

**Key Points:**
- HOCs props manipulation, conditional rendering, ‡¶¨‡¶æ additional logic ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Common use cases: Authentication, logging, data fetching‡•§
- React Redux-‡¶è‡¶∞ `connect` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º HOC‡•§

**Use case:** HOCs ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø component-‡¶è reusable logic (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® auth, error handling) inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#27._ üü£ **What is memoization in React and when should you use React.memo?**

**Memoization** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø optimization technique ‡¶Ø‡¶æ expensive calculations ‡¶¨‡¶æ renders cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React-‡¶è `React.memo` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø higher-order component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional components-‡¶ï‡ßá memoize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá props unchanged ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá re-render ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**How `React.memo` works:**
- `React.memo` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ props compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Props unchanged ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const MyComponent = React.memo(({ value }) => {
  console.log('Rendering MyComponent');
  return <div>{value}</div>;
});

const Parent = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
  return (
    <div>
      <MyComponent value="Hello" /> {/* Won't re-render if value unchanged */}
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>Count: {count}</button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**When to use `React.memo`:**
- Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ rendering expensive (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® complex UI, large lists)‡•§
- Props frequently unchanged ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- Component parent-‡¶è‡¶∞ frequent re-renders-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** `React.memo` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø unnecessary re-renders prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá large ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex components-‡¶è‡•§


### _#28._ üü£ **What are some common performance optimization techniques in React?**

React apps-‡¶è‡¶∞ performance optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common techniques:

1. **Use `React.memo`:** Functional components-‡¶è unnecessary re-renders prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
2. **useMemo & useCallback:** Expensive calculations ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function re-creation ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   const memoizedValue = useMemo(() => computeExpensiveValue(a, b), [a, b]);
   const memoizedCallback = useCallback(() => doSomething(), [deps]);
   ```
3. **Lazy Loading:** Components ‡¶¨‡¶æ routes lazily load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá (see #29).
4. **Code Splitting:** Webpack-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá dynamic imports ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá bundle size ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§
   ```jsx
   const LazyComponent = React.lazy(() => import('./LazyComponent'));
   ```
5. **Avoid Inline Functions/Objects in JSX:** Functions/objects props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá re-create ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá re-renders trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   // Bad
   <Child onClick={() => doSomething()} />
   // Good
   const handleClick = useCallback(() => doSomething(), []);
   <Child onClick={handleClick} />
   ```
6. **Use Keys in Lists:** Correct `key` prop ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá list rendering optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
7. **Profile with React DevTools:** Performance bottlenecks identify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
8. **Avoid Overusing State:** Unnecessary state updates re-renders trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Performance optimization ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø large-scale apps-‡¶è fast rendering ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç smooth user experience ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#29._ üü£ **What is lazy loading in React?**

Lazy loading ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø technique ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá components ‡¶¨‡¶æ resources (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® images, scripts) ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, initial bundle size ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ React-‡¶è `React.lazy` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Suspense` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá lazy loading implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { lazy, Suspense } from 'react';

const LazyComponent = lazy(() => import('./LazyComponent'));

const App = () => (
  <Suspense fallback={<div>Loading...</div>}>
    <LazyComponent />
  </Suspense>
);
```

**Key Points:**
- `React.lazy` dynamic imports ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá components asynchronously load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `Suspense` fallback UI ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ component load ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Routing-‡¶è (React Router) lazy loading ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ common‡•§

**Use case:** Lazy loading ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø large apps-‡¶è initial load time ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#30._ üü£ **What is React Suspense?**

React Suspense ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ asynchronous operations (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® lazy loading, data fetching) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ components ‡¶¨‡¶æ resources load ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º fallback UI ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
import { Suspense, lazy } from 'react';

const LazyComponent = lazy(() => import('./LazyComponent'));

const App = () => (
  <Suspense fallback={<div>Loading...</div>}>
    <LazyComponent />
  </Suspense>
);
```

**Key Points:**
- `Suspense` `React.lazy` ‡¶¨‡¶æ data fetching libraries (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Relay) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Concurrent rendering-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Suspense data fetching optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Multiple components ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Suspense-‡¶è wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Suspense ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø lazy-loaded components ‡¶¨‡¶æ asynchronous data fetching-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø smooth user experience ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#31._ üü£ **What is React Concurrent Mode (or React Concurrent Features)?**

React Concurrent Features (‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá Concurrent Mode ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature set ‡¶Ø‡¶æ rendering process-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ apps-‡¶ï‡ßá non-blocking rendering ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç better user experience ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Key Features:**
- **Time Slicing:** CPU-intensive renders ‡¶ï‡ßá smaller chunks-‡¶è ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Priority Scheduling:** High-priority updates (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® user input) ‡¶ï‡ßá low-priority tasks-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Suspense for Data Fetching:** Asynchronous data loading ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Example (Conceptual):**
```jsx
import { Suspense } from 'react';

const App = () => (
  <Suspense fallback={<div>Loading...</div>}>
    <DataComponent />
  </Suspense>
);
```

**Key Points:**
- Concurrent features React 18-‡¶è stable ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `startTransition` API ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá low-priority updates handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Improves performance in complex UIs with heavy state updates.

**Use case:** Concurrent features ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø large apps-‡¶è smooth animations, fast interactions, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç better performance ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#32._ üü£ **What is error boundary and how does it work?**

Error Boundary ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø special component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ child components-‡¶è‡¶∞ JavaScript errors catch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç fallback UI ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá app crash ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- Class components-‡¶è `static getDerivedStateFromError` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `componentDidCatch` implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá error boundaries ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Error ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá fallback UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç error log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
class ErrorBoundary extends React.Component {
  state = { hasError: false };

  static getDerivedStateFromError(error) {
    return { hasError: true };
  }

  componentDidCatch(error, errorInfo) {
    console.log('Error:', error, errorInfo); // Log error
  }

  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      return <h1>Something went wrong!</h1>;
    }
    return this.props.children;
  }
}

const App = () => (
  <ErrorBoundary>
    <BuggyComponent />
  </ErrorBoundary>
);
```

**Key Points:**
- Error boundaries ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ class components-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Event handlers ‡¶¨‡¶æ async code-‡¶è‡¶∞ errors catch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Production-‡¶è user-friendly error UI ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Error boundaries ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø app stability ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user experience protect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


### _#33._ üü£ **What is debouncing and throttling in React?**

**Debouncing:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function-‡¶ï‡ßá delay ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã calls ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

**Throttling:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü time interval-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example (Debouncing):**
```jsx
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import _ from 'lodash';

const Search = () => {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');

  const debouncedSearch = useCallback(
    _.debounce((value) => {
      console.log('Searching:', value); // API call here
    }, 500),
    []
  );

  const handleChange = (e) => {
    setQuery(e.target.value);
    debouncedSearch(e.target.value);
  };

  return <input value={query} onChange={handleChange} />;
};
```

**Example (Throttling):**
```jsx
import { useCallback } from 'react';
import _ from 'lodash';

const ScrollTracker = () => {
  const throttledScroll = useCallback(
    _.throttle(() => {
      console.log('Scroll position:', window.scrollY);
    }, 1000),
    []
  );

  return <div onScroll={throttledScroll}>Scroll me</div>;
};
```

**Use case:**
- **Debouncing:** Search inputs, autocomplete, ‡¶¨‡¶æ frequent user actions-‡¶è API calls ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
- **Throttling:** Scroll events, resize events, ‡¶¨‡¶æ rapid button clicks handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§


‚úÖ 5. Lifecycle & Rendering
### _#34._ üü£ **What is the component lifecycle in React?**

React-‡¶è component lifecycle ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶®‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® phase ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§: **Mounting**, **Updating**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Unmounting**‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø phase-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü events ‡¶¨‡¶æ methods ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component-‡¶è‡¶∞ creation, update, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç destruction-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

**Phases:**
1. **Mounting:** Component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM-‡¶è render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Updating:** Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¨‡¶æ props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Unmounting:** Component DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Use case:** Lifecycle ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ specific ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá logic (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® data fetching, cleanup) execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§


### _#35._ üü£ **What is the difference between mounting, updating, and unmounting?**

| **Phase**       | **Description**                                                                 | **Key Activities**                                  |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| **Mounting**    | Component ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM-‡¶è insert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§                              | Constructor, initial render, lifecycle methods (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `componentDidMount`)‡•§ |
| **Updating**    | State ‡¶¨‡¶æ props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§                              | State/props update, lifecycle methods (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `componentDidUpdate`)‡•§ |
| **Unmounting**  | Component DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§                                                | Cleanup tasks, lifecycle methods (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `componentWillUnmount`)‡•§ |

**Example:**
```jsx
class MyComponent extends React.Component {
  componentDidMount() { console.log("Mounted"); }
  componentDidUpdate() { console.log("Updated"); }
  componentWillUnmount() { console.log("Unmounted"); }
  render() { return <div>Hello</div>; }
}
```

**Use case:** Mounting-‡¶è initialization, updating-‡¶è data refresh, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unmounting-‡¶è cleanup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#36._ üü£ **What are lifecycle methods in class components (e.g., componentDidMount)?**

Lifecycle methods ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã class components-‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in methods ‡¶Ø‡¶æ lifecycle-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® phase-‡¶è automatically call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Common Lifecycle Methods:**

1. **Mounting:**
   - `constructor()`: Component initialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
   - `static getDerivedStateFromProps(props, state)`: Props ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
   - `render()`: UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
   - `componentDidMount()`: Component DOM-‡¶è add ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® API call)‡•§

2. **Updating:**
   - `static getDerivedStateFromProps(props, state)`: Props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá state update‡•§
   - `shouldComponentUpdate(nextProps, nextState)`: Re-render control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
   - `render()`: Updated UI render‡•§
   - `getSnapshotBeforeUpdate(prevProps, prevState)`: DOM update-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá snapshot capture‡•§
   - `componentDidUpdate(prevProps, prevState, snapshot)`: Update-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® DOM manipulation)‡•§

3. **Unmounting:**
   - `componentWillUnmount()`: Component remove ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá cleanup (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® timers, subscriptions)‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
class MyComponent extends React.Component {
  componentDidMount() {
    console.log("Component mounted");
  }
  componentDidUpdate(prevProps) {
    console.log("Component updated with props:", prevProps);
  }
  componentWillUnmount() {
    console.log("Component unmounting");
  }
  render() {
    return <div>Hello</div>;
  }
}
```

**Use case:** Lifecycle methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø specific lifecycle events-‡¶è logic (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® data fetching, cleanup) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#37._ üü£ **How does useEffect replace lifecycle methods?**

`useEffect` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã functional components-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ class components-‡¶è‡¶∞ lifecycle methods (`componentDidMount`, `componentDidUpdate`, `componentWillUnmount`) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it replaces:**
1. **componentDidMount:** Empty dependency array (`[]`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá `useEffect` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ mount-‡¶è run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   useEffect(() => {
     console.log("Mounted");
   }, []); // Runs once on mount
   ```

2. **componentDidUpdate:** Dependency array-‡¶è variables ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá dependencies change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   useEffect(() => {
     console.log("Updated with prop:", prop);
   }, [prop]); // Runs on prop change
   ```

3. **componentWillUnmount:** Cleanup function return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá unmount-‡¶è run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   useEffect(() => {
     const timer = setInterval(() => console.log("Timer"), 1000);
     return () => clearInterval(timer); // Cleanup on unmount
   }, []);
   ```

**Example (Combined):**
```jsx
const MyComponent = ({ prop }) => {
  useEffect(() => {
    console.log("Mounted or prop updated");
    return () => console.log("Unmounting");
  }, [prop]); // Runs on mount and prop change

  return <div>Hello</div>;
};
```

**Use case:** `useEffect` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø side effects (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® API calls, subscriptions) handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, lifecycle methods-‡¶è‡¶∞ simpler alternative ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§



### _#38._ üü£ **What is reconciliation in React?**

Reconciliation ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ process ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Virtual DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ changes detect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç real DOM-‡¶è efficiently update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ React-‡¶è‡¶∞ core mechanism, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI updates fast ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¨‡¶æ props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, React ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Previous Virtual DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (diffing)‡•§
- ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ changed parts real DOM-‡¶è update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Key Points:**
- Reconciliation Virtual DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `key` prop lists-‡¶è reconciliation optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Diffing algorithm elements-‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç position compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Reconciliation ensures minimal DOM updates, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ app performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§



### _#39._ üü£ **What is React's rendering process?**

React-‡¶è‡¶∞ rendering process ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component-‡¶è‡¶∞ UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM-‡¶è display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡•§

**Steps:**
1. **Trigger:** State ‡¶¨‡¶æ props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá rendering ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Render Phase:** Component-‡¶è‡¶∞ `render` method ‡¶¨‡¶æ function JSX return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Reconciliation:** React ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM-‡¶ï‡ßá previous-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (diffing)‡•§
4. **Commit Phase:** Changed parts real DOM-‡¶è apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
5. **Lifecycle Methods/Hooks:** `useEffect` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `componentDidMount/Update` call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const MyComponent = () => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
  useEffect(() => {
    console.log("Effect after render");
  });
  return <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>{count}</button>;
};
```
- Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `setCount` state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- React ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, reconcile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Use case:** Rendering process ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ efficient UI updates ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç side effects handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§



### _#40._ üü£ **What causes re-render in React?**

React-‡¶è re-render ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® component-‡¶è‡¶∞ state, props, ‡¶¨‡¶æ parent component-‡¶è‡¶∞ rendering change ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Causes:**
1. **State Change:** `setState` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `useState` setter call ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
   setCount(count + 1); // Triggers re-render
   ```
2. **Props Change:** Parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® props ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
   ```jsx
   <Child value={parentState} /> // parentState change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Child re-renders
   ```
3. **Parent Re-render:** Parent component re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá children by default re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Context Change:** `useContext` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `Context.Consumer` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá context value change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
5. **Hooks Dependency Change:** `useEffect`, `useMemo`, ‡¶¨‡¶æ `useCallback`-‡¶è‡¶∞ dependencies change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

**Avoid Unnecessary Re-renders:**
- `React.memo` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- `useCallback` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `useMemo` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá functions/values memoize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- Proper `key` usage lists-‡¶è‡•§

**Use case:** Re-render causes ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá optimization techniques apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§



### _#41._ üü£ **What is the virtual DOM?**

Virtual DOM ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø in-memory representation of the real DOM‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ real DOM-‡¶è‡¶∞ lightweight copy, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript object ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá UI structure store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**How it works:**
- Component render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, React Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- State/props change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Reconciliation process-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã Virtual DOM compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ changes real DOM-‡¶è apply ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example:**
```jsx
const MyComponent = () => <div>Hello</div>;
// Virtual DOM: { type: 'div', props: { children: 'Hello' } }
```

**Use case:** Virtual DOM efficient updates ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance optimization-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§



### _#42._ üü£ **What is the difference between virtual DOM and real DOM?**

| **Aspect**            | **Virtual DOM**                                              | **Real DOM**                                                |
|-----------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------|
| **Definition**        | JavaScript object ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá UI-‡¶è‡¶∞ lightweight representation‡•§  | Browser-‡¶è‡¶∞ actual DOM tree, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§             |
| **Performance**       | Fast, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ in-memory operations‡•§                            | Slower, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ direct DOM manipulation costly‡•§               |
| **Manipulation**      | React changes Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç diffs apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§             | Direct changes browser-‡¶è apply ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§                        |
| **Updates**           | Efficient, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ changed parts real DOM-‡¶è update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§        | Entire DOM update ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ slow‡•§                      |
| **Example**           | `{ type: 'div', props: { children: 'Hello' } }`            | `<div>Hello</div>`                                         |

**How it works:**
- Virtual DOM changes compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá minimal real DOM updates ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Real DOM direct manipulation browser-‡¶è‡¶∞ rendering trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
